if (!is_file('setup/sql/example_access.sql')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: setup/sql/example_access.sql');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('setup/sql/example_access.sql')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/sql/example_access.sql');
	} else if (sha1_file('setup/sql/example_access.sql') != '50d1056b5b650235463be6acf9569b23735dcf51') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/example_access.sql');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/sql/example_access.sql', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/sql/example_access.sql');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/example_access.sql') !== '50d1056b5b650235463be6acf9569b23735dcf51') {
		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/example_access.sql') !== '3a7e7fffba8526a8d23ca5a64ab32a04c5a0f09c') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/sql/example_access.sql');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/sql/example_access.sql');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/sql/example_access.sql')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/sql/example_access.sql', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/example_access.sql') !== '50d1056b5b650235463be6acf9569b23735dcf51') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/example_access.sql');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('setup/sql/example_mssql.sql')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: setup/sql/example_mssql.sql');
	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('setup/sql/example_mssql.sql')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/sql/example_mssql.sql');
	} else if (sha1_file('setup/sql/example_mssql.sql') != '2272b3efcea154e919c065e693345895cecd25fa') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/example_mssql.sql');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/sql/example_mssql.sql', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/sql/example_mssql.sql');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/example_mssql.sql') !== '2272b3efcea154e919c065e693345895cecd25fa') {
		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/example_mssql.sql') !== 'ae85c287f0c2afd3233df18f078f17babc682095') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/sql/example_mssql.sql');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/sql/example_mssql.sql');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/sql/example_mssql.sql')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/sql/example_mssql.sql', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/example_mssql.sql') !== '2272b3efcea154e919c065e693345895cecd25fa') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/example_mssql.sql');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('setup/sql/example_mysql.sql')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: setup/sql/example_mysql.sql');
	writefile_3();
	if (!is_file('setup/sql/example_mysql.sql')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/sql/example_mysql.sql');
	} else if (sha1_file('setup/sql/example_mysql.sql') != '8ae1fb7c0879ff288771e213b2c87739d04062f2') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/example_mysql.sql');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/sql/example_mysql.sql', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/sql/example_mysql.sql');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/example_mysql.sql') !== '8ae1fb7c0879ff288771e213b2c87739d04062f2') {
		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/example_mysql.sql') !== 'e15da8f34bfa1771932d34cf7e77857fdee4b569') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/sql/example_mysql.sql');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/sql/example_mysql.sql');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/sql/example_mysql.sql')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/sql/example_mysql.sql', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/example_mysql.sql') !== '8ae1fb7c0879ff288771e213b2c87739d04062f2') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/example_mysql.sql');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('setup/sql/example_oracle.sql')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: setup/sql/example_oracle.sql');
	writefile_4();
	if (!is_file('setup/sql/example_oracle.sql')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/sql/example_oracle.sql');
	} else if (sha1_file('setup/sql/example_oracle.sql') != '08924543352136fb7a3881e85b8ac834286035c7') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/example_oracle.sql');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/sql/example_oracle.sql', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/sql/example_oracle.sql');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/example_oracle.sql') !== '08924543352136fb7a3881e85b8ac834286035c7') {
		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/example_oracle.sql') !== '091ce987066dc69389392068edd10c1a14f47f58') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/sql/example_oracle.sql');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/sql/example_oracle.sql');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/sql/example_oracle.sql')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/sql/example_oracle.sql', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/example_oracle.sql') !== '08924543352136fb7a3881e85b8ac834286035c7') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/example_oracle.sql');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('setup/sql/example_pgsql.sql')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: setup/sql/example_pgsql.sql');
	writefile_5();
	if (!is_file('setup/sql/example_pgsql.sql')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/sql/example_pgsql.sql');
	} else if (sha1_file('setup/sql/example_pgsql.sql') != 'edf3443e1f747a139d731eae0e020de644d45a18') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/example_pgsql.sql');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/sql/example_pgsql.sql', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/sql/example_pgsql.sql');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/example_pgsql.sql') !== 'edf3443e1f747a139d731eae0e020de644d45a18') {
		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/example_pgsql.sql') !== 'af6a9fdc698a9359d0cae4ea80e6bbfd2d4f8711') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/sql/example_pgsql.sql');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/sql/example_pgsql.sql');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/sql/example_pgsql.sql')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/sql/example_pgsql.sql', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_5();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/example_pgsql.sql') !== 'edf3443e1f747a139d731eae0e020de644d45a18') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/example_pgsql.sql');
		}
	}
}

		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/sql/example_sqlite.sql');
	} else if (sha1_file('setup/sql/example_sqlite.sql') != 'd134f029ddcb542759b1c1d41cf587ed94277ee0') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/example_sqlite.sql');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/sql/example_sqlite.sql', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/sql/example_sqlite.sql');

			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/sql/example_sqlite.sql');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/sql/example_sqlite.sql');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/sql/example_sqlite.sql')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/sql/example_sqlite.sql', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_6();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/example_sqlite.sql') !== 'd134f029ddcb542759b1c1d41cf587ed94277ee0') {
